5 
PART 1:  INTRODUCTION 
 
 
CLAUSE 1: TITLE OF THIS SCHEME 
 
This Scheme shall be known as the Tshwane Land Use Scheme, 2024 (TLUS 2024), hereafter referred 
to as “the Scheme” or “this Scheme”, as Adopted by virtue of Notice LA 652 of 2024, dated 8 May 2024, 
which shall be applicable to all Land and Buildings within the area of jurisdiction of the City of Tshwane 
Metropolitan Municipality.  
 
 
CLAUSE 2: RESPONSIBLE AUTHORITY 
 
The City of Tshwane Metropolitan Municipality is the authority responsible for enforcing and bringing 
into effect the provisions of this Scheme read with the Corporate System of Delegations in terms of 
section 59 of the Local Government: Municipal Systems Act, 2000 (Act 32 of 2000), sections 35 and 56 
of the Spatial Planning and Land Use Management Act, 2013 (Act 16 of 2013) (SPLUMA) and sections 
15 and 25 of the City of Tshwane Land Use Management (LUM) By-law, 2016 (Amended 2024), as 
may be amended from time to time. 
 
 
CLAUSE 3: COMPONENTS AND INTERPRETATION OF THIS SCHEME 
 
(1)   This Scheme is divided into parts relating to the following matters: 
 
PART 1:  INTRODUCTION 
PART 2:  STREETS AND BUILDING LINES 
PART 3:  USE OF LAND AND BUILDINGS 
PART 4:  DEVELOPMENT CONDITIONS 
PART 5:  PARKING AND LOADING FACILITIES 
PART 6:  ENVIRONMENTAL AMENITY AND APPEARANCE OF BUILDINGS 
PART 7:  GENERAL CONDITIONS 
PART 8:  SCHEDULES 
 
(2)   Annexures L, as defined hereafter.  
 
(3)   Conversion Tables, as defined hereafter. 
 
(4)   Diagrams as part of the Clauses and Schedules hereafter. 
 
(5)   Electronic Zoning Database, as defined hereafter. 
 
(6)   Land Use Scheme Register, as defined hereafter. 
 
(7)   Scheme Map, as defined hereafter. 
 
(8)   Tables as part of the Clauses. 
 
(9)   The use and interpretation of the Scheme shall be determined by the Municipality and shall be 
enforced in the following manner: 
 
(a)   The Municipality’s interpretation of the Clauses and Schedules shall prevail.  
 
(b)   The headings and numbering of the Scheme are for reference purposes only and do not 
constitute any provisions of the Scheme.  

 
 
TSHWANE LAND USE SCHEME, 2024 
 
Adopted by virtue of Notice LA 652 of 2024:  08 May 2024  
Comes into operation:  01 July 2024 
                                                                             
 
 
6 
 
(c)   On Adoption, this Scheme will be published in English. Should any dispute arise as to the 
content thereof, this shall be regarded as the official version of the Scheme Adopted by 
the Municipality. Upon request to the Municipality, the Scheme may be provided either 
wholly  or  in  part  in  any of  the  languages  approved  by  the Municipality  as the  official 
languages  of  communication  within  its  jurisdiction.  The  version  of  the  Scheme  of  the 
Municipality’s Language Services Section shall be subject to technical verification from the 
Economic  Development  and  Spatial  Planning  Department  or  an  entity  within  the 
Municipality  responsible  for  the  administration  of  land  use  management  and  shall  be 
provided within the capacity and resources of the Municipality.  
 
 
CLAUSE 4: TRANSITIONAL ARRANGEMENTS 
 
(1)   Any Adopted Land Development Application in terms of the provisions of a land use scheme or 
town-planning scheme in operation for: 
 
(a)   the erection or use of Buildings; and/or  
(b)   for the use of Land; and/or  
(c)   any rights legally exercised in terms of such scheme;  
 
before the Adoption date of this Scheme, as contemplated in Clause 1, shall be deemed to be a 
Land Development Application, in terms of the provisions of this Scheme, provided that any such 
land use rights obtained through such Land Development Application, shall continue to be in force 
and effect, subject to the provisions of the relevant legislation in terms of which it was approved. 
 
(2)   Any Land Development Application that has been granted, approved or adopted, including any 
documentation, permissions, consent uses, annexures or schedules, in terms of any former town-
planning scheme and/or land use and development control measures in terms of any legislation, 
in operation or applicable within the Municipality or other rights granted or promulgated in terms 
of  other  applicable  land  use  legislation  read  with  Subclause  (1)  above,  prior  to  the 
commencement of this Scheme, shall be deemed to have been granted, approved or Adopted in 
terms of this Scheme.  
 
(3)   Any Land Development Application that has been granted, approved or adopted, in terms of a 
town-planning scheme in operation prior to the commencement of this Scheme as contemplated 
in Subclause (2) above, shall be interpreted by the Municipality with reference to the land use 
rights as contained and defined in terms of this Scheme, provided that in the interpretation of the 
land use  rights  in  terms  of  this  Scheme,  no  land  use  rights  may  materially be amended or 
removed and/or reduced, nor may any additional rights be granted through such interpretation, 
read with the Guideline as contemplated in section 12(3) of the LUM By-law. 
 
(4)   Where any Land Development Application on the date of commencement of this Scheme is 
pending (not approved) before the Municipality in terms of a town-planning scheme that was in 
operation within the jurisdiction of the Municipality, which is substituted by this Scheme, then the 
application(s) in terms of that scheme and the scheme documentation related to that application, 
shall be finalised in terms of the provisions of this Scheme, in accordance with the type of Land 
Development Application as contemplated in this Scheme, read with Subclause (3) above, and 
further read with section 10(1) of the LUM By-law and section 24 and 26(1)(b) of the Act. 
 
(5)   Where any Land Development Application on the date of commencement of this Scheme is 
pending (approved but not Adopted) before the Municipality in terms of a town-planning scheme 
that  was  in  operation  within  the  jurisdiction  of  the  Municipality,  which  is  substituted  by  this 
Scheme, where in the opinion of the Municipality such application may be finalised in terms of 
that  scheme  in  terms  of  which  it  was  submitted,  the  scheme  documents  related  to  those 
applications shall be incorporated into this Scheme, read with section 10(1) of the LUM By-law 
and section 24 and 26(1)(b) of the Act. 

 
 
TSHWANE LAND USE SCHEME, 2024 
 
Adopted by virtue of Notice LA 652 of 2024:  08 May 2024  
Comes into operation:  01 July 2024 
                                                                             
 
 
7 
 
(6)   Where any Land Development Application on the date of commencement of this Scheme is 
pending (not approved, or approved but not Adopted) before the Municipality in terms of a town-
planning scheme that was in operation within the jurisdiction of the Municipality, substituted by 
this Scheme, where in the opinion of the Municipality such application would not be capable of 
being submitted in terms of this Scheme, such application shall be finalised in terms of that 
scheme, and shall be incorporated into this Scheme, in such a manner as to not create or amend 
land use rights other than those which were approved as an exemption due to the assumption 
against retrospectivity.  
 
(7)   The  Guideline  in  terms  of  section  12(3)  of  the  LUM  By-law,  contains  tables,  referred  to  as 
Conversion Tables which shall be used for the conversion and/or interpretation of all documents, 
zoning, clauses, schedules and annexures prepared and approved in terms of town-planning 
schemes  in  operation  prior  to  the  commencement  of  this  Scheme  and  in  accordance  with 
processes  as  contemplated  in  the  LUM  By-law,  where  such  by-law  makes  provision  for 
applications in terms of this Scheme. 
 
(8)   The transitional arrangements as set out in sections 2 and 3 of the LUM By-law shall apply mutatis 
mutandis. 
 
 
CLAUSE 5: DEFINITIONS 
 
Introduction to the definitions of the Scheme 
 
The definitions have been categorised into two sections, being: 
 
-     definitions of terminology that are used in the Scheme; and 
 
-     definitions of land use rights that define the specific use of Land and Buildings. 
 
In  this  Scheme,  except  where  the  context  otherwise  indicates  or  where  it  is  otherwise  expressly 
provided for, the following words and expressions have the respective meanings hereinafter assigned 
to them and any other word or expression to which a meaning has been assigned in the LUM By-law 
shall bear that meaning. Definitions that are not contained in Clause 5, shall revert to the definitions as 
contained in the LUM By-law. 
 
In the text of this Scheme terminology that has been defined in this Scheme shall be capitalised for 
identification purposes. Should a dispute arise on whether the definition of any terminology or specific 
use apply or not due to capitalization, the interpretation of the Municipality shall prevail.   
 
 
DEFINITIONS OF TERMINOLOGY 
 
 
A 
 
ACT 
Means the Spatial Planning and Land Use Management Act, 2013 (Act 16 of 2013) as may be amended 
from time to time.  
 
ADJOINING OWNER(S) 
Means adjoining owner(s) as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
ADOPT/ADOPTED 
Means adopt or adopted as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 

 
 
TSHWANE LAND USE SCHEME, 2024 
 
Adopted by virtue of Notice LA 652 of 2024:  08 May 2024  
Comes into operation:  01 July 2024 
                                                                             
 
 
8 
 
AGRICULTURAL HOLDING 
Means land as set out in terms of the Agricultural Holdings (Transvaal) Registration Act, 1919 (Act 22 
of 1919) as may be amended from time to time.  
 
AMENDMENT SCHEME 
Means amendment scheme as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
ANCILLARY AND SUBSERVIENT  
Means the use of Land and Buildings for purposes which, in the opinion of the Municipality, support and 
compliment the main permitted use on the Property and which shall not be exercised as separate or 
independent  uses  on  the  Property  in  the  event  that  the  main  permitted  use  on  the  Property  is 
discontinued or is rendered incapable of being exercised. 
 
ANNEXURE L 
Means the set of documents showing those restrictions and measures intended to control and limit the 
exercising of land use rights and related details of the Adopted land use rights permitted, including the 
conditions imposed on certain Properties marked with a black number within a black circle on the 
Scheme Map, which rights and conditions shall prevail over any default Clauses or provisions of the 
Scheme relating to such restrictions and measures, provided that, if land use rights and conditions are 
not stipulated in such set of documents, the default provisions of the Scheme Clauses shall apply as 
read with Clause 4 and include any Adopted annexures or schedules of a former town-planning scheme 
applicable in the Municipal area. 
 
APPLICANT  
Means applicant as contemplated in the LUM By-law.  
 
AUTHORISED OFFICIAL 
Means authorised official as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
AVERAGE GROUND LEVEL 
(1)   Means the average between the highest and lowest point of the Natural Ground Level on a 
Property. 
 
(2)   Clause 26 shall be applicable. 
 
 
B 
 
BASEMENT 
(1)   Means any part of a Building below the Average Ground Level of which no part is more than one 
(1) metre above such average level. 
 
(2)   Clauses 9(4), 12 and 26 shall be applicable. 
 
BENEFICIAL OWNER 
Means beneficial owner as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
BUILDING 
Means a building as contemplated in the National Building Regulations and Building Standards Act, 
1977 (Act 103 of 1977) (NBR) as may be amended from time to time. 
 
BUILDING LINE  
Means an imaginary line on a Property that demarcates the boundary of the Building Restriction Area 
and is at a fixed distance from any boundary of such Property measured in metres.  
 

 
 
TSHWANE LAND USE SCHEME, 2024 
 
Adopted by virtue of Notice LA 652 of 2024:  08 May 2024  
Comes into operation:  01 July 2024 
                                                                             
 
 
9 
 
BUILDING RESTRICTION AREA  
Means the area on a Property where no Building, except as permitted by the Scheme, may be erected 
and which is bounded on one side by a Building Line and on the other side by a boundary of the Property. 
 
BY-LAWS 
Means the Municipal by-laws in force within the area of jurisdiction of the Scheme, as may be amended 
from time to time. 
 
 
C 
 
CANOPY 
(1)   Means a cantilevered or suspended Roof or slab which is not enclosed and may project from the 
wall of a Building. 
 
(2)   Clause 10 shall be applicable. 
 
CLAUSES 
Means clauses in the Scheme applicable to Land, Buildings and Properties within the Scheme Area. 
 
CONDITIONS OF APPROVAL 
Means conditions of approval as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
CONSENT USE 
(1)   Means the use of Land and Buildings granted in addition to the primary land use right(s) by the 
Municipality, subject to Clause 16 of the Scheme, read with the provisions of the LUM By-law 
and shall be subject to Conditions of Approval.  
 
(2)   Conditions of Approval may be contained in different documents and formats, for example, a 
letter, a document in tabular format or an approval document.  
 
(3)   Consent Uses Adopted in terms of this Scheme, shall be referred to as a Consent Use Scheme 
Document. 
 
CONSERVATION 
(1)   Means the protection, maintenance and sustainable use of Land and Buildings in terms of its 
natural, cultural, historical or built environmental significance, with the objective to preserve the 
identified special characteristics, whether set apart as such by legislation or not. 
 
(2)   The  Land,  Properties  or  Buildings  need  special  management  and  maintenance  in  order  to 
preserve the identified natural, historical or cultural characteristics, these include, but are not 
limited to, ridges, watercourses, wetlands and sensitive eco-systems, heritage sites, historical 
Buildings or sites of cultural significance. 
 
(3)   Such Land, Properties or Buildings may be identified by the Municipality from time to time or are 
determined  through  the  National  Heritage  Resources  Act,  1999  (Act  25  of  1999)  (NHRA), 
National Environmental Management Act, 1998 (Act 107 of 1998) as may be amended from time 
to  time  or  other  related  national  and  provincial  legislation  pertaining  to  biodiversity  in  the 
establishment of protected areas. 
 
CONTROLLING AUTHORITY 
Means the controlling authority as contemplated in section 1 of the Advertising on Roads and Ribbon 
Development Act, 1940 (Act 21 of 1940) or the Commission as defined in section 1 of the National 
Roads Act, 1971 (Act 54 of 1971) or the Gauteng Transport Infrastructure Act, 2001 (Act 8 of 2001) as 

 
 
TSHWANE LAND USE SCHEME, 2024 
 
Adopted by virtue of Notice LA 652 of 2024:  08 May 2024  
Comes into operation:  01 July 2024 
                                                                             
 
 
10
may be amended from time to time read with section 45(6) of the Act and the provisions of the LUM By-
law. 
 
CONVERSION TABLES  
Means a set of tables used for the conversion of the content of documents, zoning, clauses, schedules 
and annexures from former town-planning schemes as well as the Tshwane Town-planning Scheme, 
2008 (revised 2014), and other land use legislation to this Scheme as contemplated in Schedule 18, 
read with Clause 4(5) of this Scheme. Conversion Tables form part of the “Guidelines”, as contemplated 
in section 12(3) of the LUM By-law.  
 
COVERAGE  
(1)   Means the percentage of the area of a Property, including any servitude area and Panhandle area 
covered by the roofed area of all Buildings on the Property, as seen vertically from above, but it 
does not include a Building without a Roof.  
 
(2)   Clause 27 shall be applicable. 
 
COVERAGE ZONE 
Means a specific zone in Table E indicating the Coverage applicable to a Property reflected in the 
Scheme and/or Electronic Zoning Database of the Municipality. 
 
 
D 
 
DENSITY 
Means the number of Dwelling Houses or Dwelling Units permitted on a Property under the respective 
Use Zones: 
 
(1)   on an Erf zoned Residential 1, the number of Dwelling Houses captured on the Electronic Zoning 
Database (Schedule 6). Clause 20 shall be applicable;  
 
(2)   on a Property zoned Residential 2, the number of Dwelling Units expressed in terms of Dwelling 
Units per hectare or otherwise stated. Clause 21 shall be applicable; and 
 
(3)   on Properties zoned Residential 3, Residential 4 or Special for Dwelling Units, the number of 
Dwelling Units per hectare may be specified only for the purposes of calculation of contributions 
for engineering services. 
 
DESIGNATED AREAS 
Means designated areas as contemplated in section 21 (k) and (l)(ii) of the Act and includes townships, 
informal settlements, communal land which are typically former homeland areas, or areas under tribal 
leadership and areas characterised by widespread poverty and deprivation as referred to in section 7(a) 
of the Act. 
 
 
E 
 
ELECTRONIC ZONING DATABASE 
(1)   Means  the  database  of the  Municipality, where  the  Zoning  data  of  the  Scheme  is captured 
electronically and updated. 
 
(2)   Data extracted from this database may be used for purposes of, but not limited to: 
(a)   Zoning Certificates; 
(b)   compilation of maps; and  
(c)   research. 

 
 
TSHWANE LAND USE SCHEME, 2024 
 
Adopted by virtue of Notice LA 652 of 2024:  08 May 2024  
Comes into operation:  01 July 2024 
                                                                             
 
 
11
 
ERF 
Means an erf as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
EXISTING GROUND LEVEL 
(1)   Means the natural or disturbed topography and the level of a Property, after the installation of all 
necessary engineering services required to service a township or development area, which may 
be used for measuring the Average Ground Level and the Height of a Building. 
 
(2)   The Municipality may require the certification of the Existing Ground Level to its satisfaction, prior 
to the approval of a Land Development Application, Site Development Plan or building plans. 
 
(3)   Clause 26 shall be applicable. 
 
EXISTING USE 
Means the lawful use of Land and Buildings, subject to section 3(3) of the LUM By-law.  
 
 
F 
 
FLOOD LINE 
Means the flood line as defined in section 144 of the National Water Act, 1998 (Act 36 of 1998) as may 
be amended from time to time, including any other flood line that the Municipality may require and shall 
be  reflected  or  indicated  on  the  Scheme  Map  or  other  documents  related  to  Land  Development 
Applications, where applicable. 
 
FLOOR AREA RATIO (FAR) 
(1)   Means the ratio of the Gross Floor Area (GFA) of a Building to the total area of the Property, 
including any servitudes, on which such a Building is erected or is to be erected, that is:  
 
 
 
 
 
(2)   Clause 25 shall be applicable. 
 
FLOOR AREA RATIO ZONE  
Means a specific zone in Table C indicating the FAR applicable to a Property reflected in the Scheme 
and/or Electronic Zoning Database of the Municipality.  
 
FUNCTIONAL OPEN SPACE  
As defined in the LUM By-law. 
 
 
G 
 
GENERAL PLAN 
Means general plan as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
GROSS FLOOR AREA (GFA) 
Means the area of a Building which is determined by multiplying the area of the Property by the FAR.  
 
 
 
 
                     Gross Floor Area     
FAR     =    Area of the Property 

 
 
TSHWANE LAND USE SCHEME, 2024 
 
Adopted by virtue of Notice LA 652 of 2024:  08 May 2024  
Comes into operation:  01 July 2024 
                                                                             
 
 
12
GROUND FLOOR 
(1)   Means the floor of a Building which is at or closest to the Natural Ground Level of the Property 
on which such Building may be or has been erected and excludes a Basement and shall be the 
first Storey in the calculation of Height. 
 
(2)   Clause 26 shall be applicable. 
 
GUEST 
Means a person lodging in accommodation for a short period away from their normal place of permanent 
residence. 
 
GUIDELINE 
Means guideline as contemplated in section 12(3) of the LUM By-law. 
 
 
H 
 
HABITABLE ROOM 
Means a room designed or used for human habitation according to the minimum standards prescribed 
in the NBR, but shall not include a storeroom, Kitchen, scullery, toilet, bathroom or a passage.  
 
HEIGHT 
(1)   Means the height of any part of a Building as measured vertically from the Natural Ground Level 
at the footprint of the Building to the highest point of the Building, provided that a maximum of 
500 mm of fill above the Natural Ground Level, for storm water management, shall be excluded 
from the height calculation. 
 
(2)   Clause 26 shall be applicable.  
 
HEIGHT ZONE  
Means a specific zone in Table D indicating the Height applicable to a Property reflected in the Scheme 
and/or Electronic Zoning Database of the Municipality.  
 
 
I 
 
ILLEGAL TOWNSHIP 
Means illegal township as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
 
J 
 
None 
 
 
K 
 
KITCHEN 
Means a room or part of a room designed or used for the storage of food, utensils, crockery, cutlery and 
for the preparation of food and may include washing facilities or have interleading washing facilities. 
 
 
 

 
 
TSHWANE LAND USE SCHEME, 2024 
 
Adopted by virtue of Notice LA 652 of 2024:  08 May 2024  
Comes into operation:  01 July 2024 
                                                                             
 
 
13
KITCHENETTE 
(1)   Means an area designed or used as a Kitchen in a Habitable Room not exceeding 20% of the 
floor area of such room, which area shall be calculated as follows: 
 
(1,0 metre working top width) x (length of working top/sink + length of any floor 
standing kitchen unit or kitchen appliance).  
 
(2)   Schedule 7, Diagram 13, shall be applicable. 
 
 
L 
 
LAND 
Means land as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
LAND DEVELOPMENT APPLICATION  
Means a land development application as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
LANDSCAPE DEVELOPMENT PLAN 
Means a plan containing information on existing natural features and vegetation and proposed soft and 
hard landscaping, including the design information specifying species, quantities and qualities of the 
plants, or such other information as the Municipality may require, subject to Clause 31. 
 
LAND USE MANAGEMENT BY-LAW (LUM BY-LAW) 
Means  the  City  of  Tshwane  Land  Use  Management  By-law,  2016  (Amended  2024),  as  may  be 
amended from time to time. 
 
LAND USE SCHEME REGISTER (LUS REGISTER) 
Means the LUS Register as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
LINE OF NO ACCESS  
Means a line of no access as contemplated in Clause 7(2). 
 
 
LOCAL AUTHORITY 
Means Municipality as defined.  
 
LOFT 
Means a Storey in the Roof of a Building which may be used for the same purposes as the other Storeys 
in the same Building and which shall be calculated as FAR and Height in terms of Clauses 25 and 26, 
respectively, or as stipulated in an Annexure L or any other Scheme document. 
 
 
M 
 
MEZZANINE FLOOR 
Means an intermediate floor between two (2) main floors, or the floor and ceiling, of a Building, the area 
of which does not exceed 25% of the floor area of the same room below it. 
 
MINIMUM ERF SIZE 
Means the minimum size of an Erf zoned Residential 1, expressed in square metres, for purposes of 
considering a subdivision and is captured on the Electronic Zoning Database (Schedule 6). 
 
MUNICIPAL APPEALS TRIBUNAL  
Means the Municipal Appeals Tribunal as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 

 
 
TSHWANE LAND USE SCHEME, 2024 
 
Adopted by virtue of Notice LA 652 of 2024:  08 May 2024  
Comes into operation:  01 July 2024 
                                                                             
 
 
14
 
MUNICIPAL PLANNING TRIBUNAL  
Means the Municipal Planning Tribunal as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
MUNICIPALITY 
Means the Municipality as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
 
N 
 
NATURAL AREAS 
Means natural areas as contemplated in the LUM By-law 
 
NATURAL GROUND LEVEL 
 
(1)   Means the natural topography and the original level of the ground of the Property before it was 
mechanically disturbed through excavations or where filling takes place and is the level which is 
used for measuring the Height of a Building. 
 
(2)   The Municipality may require the certification of the Natural Ground Level, to the satisfaction of 
the Municipality. 
 
(3)   Clause 26 shall be applicable. 
 
NBR 
Means the National Building Regulations and Building Standards Act, 1977 (Act 103 of 1977) as may 
be amended from time to time.  
 
NET FLOOR AREA (NFA) 
Means the area of a Building determined by the deduction of certain floor areas from the Gross Floor 
Area as provided for in Schedule 7. 
 
NOTARIAL TIE 
Means the linking of two (2) or more contiguous Properties by means of a notarial agreement registered 
as such in an appropriate notarial deed in the offices of the Registrar of Deeds and recorded against 
the title deeds of the Properties, which form the subject of the notarial tie agreement and which also 
joins the Municipality as a party to the tie agreement with the aim of creating a single land parcel, which 
for judicial purposes may be dealt with in accordance with the notarial agreement for development 
purposes, but shall not create a single or uniform zoning over the Properties unless specified as such 
in an Annexure L, provided that: 
 
(1)   where  Properties  are  not  contiguous,  the  Municipality  may  in  its  sole  discretion  allow  the 
registration of a notarial tie, where as a result of the tie agreement the land use rights may be 
exercised on both or all the Properties, in such a manner that does not contravene the land use 
rights on each of the Properties; and 
 
(2)   where Properties are registered in the offices of the  Registrar of Deeds as an  Erf, lot, plot, 
Agricultural  Holding, sectional title sections  or  farm  portions,  a  notarial  tie  between  different 
statuses of registration may not be permitted. 
 
NOTICE  
Means notice as contemplated in the LUM By-law.

15
O 
 
OCCUPANT 
Means any Person in physical or lawful occupation of any Land or Building or Property without regard 
to the legal means by which such Person occupies such Property.   
 
OWNER 
Means owner as contemplated in the LUM By-law. 
 
 
P 
 
PANHANDLE 
Means that part of a Property, which is – 
 
(1)   a minimum of three (3) metres wide and a maximum of eight (8) metres wide; and 
 
(2)   used exclusively as access to a Street. 
 
PANHANDLE PROPERTY 
Means a Property consisting of a part used exclusively as a Panhandle and a part used for the erection 
of Buildings.  
 
PARKING SPACE 
(1)   Means an area, the dimensions of which area shall be a minimum of 2,5 metres wide and a 
minimum of five (5) metres long, used exclusively for the parking of a vehicle not being for trade 
or sale.  
 
(2)   Access or manoeuvring space, ramps or columns shall be excluded. 
 
PERMISSION 
(1)    Means the permission granted by the Municipality in terms of Clause 15 thereof permitting the 
use of Land and Building for a specific purpose or to permit a relaxation of a condition applicable 
to the use of a Land or Building and such permission may be made subject to Conditions of 
Approval. 
 
(2)   Conditions  of  Approval  may  be  contained  in  different  formats  depending  on  the  type  of 
Permission, for example, an approval note on a building plan, a letter, a document in tabular 
format or an approval document.  
 
(3)   Permissions granted in terms of this Scheme, shall be referred to as a Permission Scheme 
Document. 
 
PERSON 
Means person as contemplated in the LUM By-law.  
 
PHYSICAL BARRIER 
(1)   Means a permanently fixed structure intended as a barrier erected on the boundary of a Property. 
 
(2)   Clause 18(3) shall be applicable. 
 
PRIVATE INFRASTRUCTURE SERVICES  
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for infrastructure and engineering services, which infrastructure 
is controlled, managed, provided and maintained by a private person or body other than an organ

Comes into operation:  01 July 2024 
                                                                             
 
 
16
of state for the use and benefit of a group of people lawfully linked to the provision of such 
infrastructure through ownership or members.  
 
(2)   Private  Infrastructure  Services  may  include,  but  is  not  limited  to,  infrastructure  services  for 
telecommunication masts, energy generation, rooftop antennae, storm water attenuation and 
wastewater treatment facilities, for use by private persons or bodies or for such persons as 
determined  by  the  Municipality  which  may  include  infrastructure  or  engineering  services, 
provided  to  the  general  public  read  with  paragraph  (1)(j)  of  the  definition  of  Public  Service 
Infrastructure. 
 
(3)   Clauses 14(8) and 26(7) shall be applicable.  
 
PROPERTY(IES) 
Means property(ies) as contemplated in the LUM By-law.  
 
PUBLIC SERVICE INFRASTRUCTURE 
(1)   Means  Land and  Buildings  used  for  infrastructure  which  has  been  or  are  to  be  installed  or 
constructed by an organ of state or private person or body, whether owned by an organ of state 
or a private person or body, for the use and benefit of the general public in the opinion of the 
Municipality and which includes such infrastructure that is used by or to which the general public 
links or a Property owned by a member of the public is linked or have access, including the 
following, but not limited to: 
 
(a)   National Roads, Provincial Roads or  other Public Roads  on which goods, services or 
labour move across a municipal boundary; 
 
(b)   water and sewer systems including, pipes, ducts or other conduits, dams, Reservoirs, 
Sewerage Works, water treatment plants or water pumps forming part of a water and sewer 
system; 
 
(c)   Solar Power Plant, Power Stations, power substations or power lines forming part of an 
electricity scheme serving the public, including alternative energy provisions systems as 
may be determined by the Municipality from time to time and through energy efficiency 
legislation; 
 
(d)   Biofuel Plant or refineries or pipelines for gas or liquid fuel, forming part of a scheme for 
transporting such fuel; 
 
(e)   railway lines forming part of a national railway system; 
 
(f)    communication towers, telecommunication masts, exchange or lines whether constructed 
or installed below or above ground, forming part of communication system serving the 
public, Telecommunication Centre and Telecommunication Services; 
 
(g)   runways, aprons and air traffic control units at national or provincial Airports or privately 
operated Airports as may be determined by the Municipality, including the vacant Land 
known  as  the  obstacle  free  zone  surrounding  these,  which  must  be  vacant  for  air 
navigation purposes; 
 
(h)   any other public controlled infrastructure as may be prescribed;  
 
(i)    a real right in favour of the general public or from which the public benefits or has access 
to, registered against immovable Property in connection with infrastructure contemplated 
in (a) to (h) above; and

(j)    may  include  Private Infrastructure  Services  classified  as  Public  Service  Infrastructure, 
which in the opinion of the Municipality has been constructed and/or installed, maintained, 
owned and operated by a private person or body for the benefit of the general public. 
 
(2)   Clause 14(8) shall be applicable. 
 
 
Q 
 
None 
 
 
R 
 
REAR BOUNDARY 
Means any boundary of a Property opposite to a Street Boundary, provided that, where a Property has 
two or more Street Boundaries, the boundaries opposite to such Street Boundaries shall be regarded as 
the Side Boundaries. 
 
REAR BUILDING LINE 
Means a Building Line applicable to the Rear Boundary of a Property.  
 
ROOF  
Means the external upper covering of a Building which includes all roof type materials. 
 
 
S 
 
SCHEDULE 
Means the schedules in this Scheme setting out inter alia the provisions applicable to the Zoning and 
Clauses of the Scheme. 
 
SCHEME 
Means scheme as contemplated in Clause 1. 
 
SCHEME AREA 
Means the area to which the Scheme is applicable which corresponds with the demarcated Municipal 
boundaries as indicated on the Scheme Map. 
 
SCHEME MAP  
Means a map depicting the Zoning in the Scheme Area and which may be electronically represented 
and may be provided by any means available to the satisfaction of the Municipality. 
 
SIDE BOUNDARY 
Means a boundary other than the Street Boundary or the Rear Boundary in relation to a Property. 
 
SIDE BUILDING LINE 
Means a Building Line applicable to the Side Boundary of a Property.  
 
SIGN 
Means an advertising sign as contemplated in the By-laws for the Control of Outdoor Advertising, 2006, 
as may be amended or replaced from time to time.

18
SITE DEVELOPMENT PLAN 
Means a plan as prescribed and contemplated in Clause 31.  
 
SPECIAL DEVELOPMENT AREAS  
(1)   Means defined areas where specific stipulations and conditions are applicable. 
 
(2)   Special Development Areas may include but are not limited to: 
(a)   density restrictions for certain areas; 
(b)   development control zones for Coverage, Floor Area Ratio and Height; 
(c)   development incentives; 
(d)   Height restrictions for certain areas; 
(e)   historical Conservation and heritage sites according to the National Heritage Resources 
Act, 1999 (NHRA); 
(f)    inclusionary housing; 
(g)   nature Conservation;  
(h)   parking requirements and relaxation;  
(i)    protected areas; and 
(j)    urban renewal. 
 
(3)   Designated Areas shall be excluded.  
 
STOREY  
(1)   Means that part of a Building, included between the surface of any floor and the surface of the 
next floor above, or if there is no floor above it, then up to the ceiling of a Building, provided that: 
 
(a)   in counting the number of Storeys of a Building, the Ground Floor is the first Storey and 
the next floor above is the second Storey; 
 
(b)   any Mezzanine Floor, open walk floor, catwalk or gallery shall be considered to be part of 
the Storey in which it is situated; and 
 
(c)   a Basement does not constitute a Storey. 
 
(2)   Clause 26 shall be applicable. 
 
STREET BOUNDARY 
Means the common boundary between a Property and a Street, National Roads and Provincial Roads. 
 
STREET BUILDING LINE 
Means a Building Line applicable to the Street Boundary of a Property. 
 
STRUCTURE 
Means a Building as defined. 
 
 
T 
 
None 
 
 
U 
 
USE ZONE  
Means categories of land use zoning indicated in Clause 14, Table B.

ZONING CERTIFICATE

(2)   Zoning Certificate may include the Zoning, land uses, development controls and may further 
include adopted Consent Uses and Permissions, as may be available, to be provided by the 
Municipality 
 
 
DEFINITIONS OF LAND USE RIGHTS 
 
 
A 
 
ABATTOIR 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used to slaughter animals and poultry and may include Ancillary and 
Subservient processing associated therewith, packaging and sale of animal and poultry products.  
 
(2)   Schedule 8 shall be applicable. 
 
ACCESS CONTROL 
Means Land and Buildings used for purposes of controlling access to a Property including a security 
gate, Guard House and may include Ancillary and Subservient uses, such as an Office, to control 
access to or from a Street.

20
 
ADDITIONAL DWELLING HOUSE 
Means one (1) additional Dwelling House, subject to Clause 14(10). 
 
ADULT PREMISES  
Means a Shop for the sale of goods and material of an explicit sexual nature, including the distribution 
or exhibition of films or videos which are classified as "X18" or "R18" in terms of the provisions of the 
Films and Publications Amendment Act, 2019 (Act 11 of 2019) as may be amended from time to time. 
 
AGRICULTURAL INDUSTRY 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for any farming activity such as, but not limited to, piggery, 
poultry farming and cattle feeding lots, that is performed on such a scale and with such intensity 
that it could possibly cause a health nuisance in respect of noise, smells, waste and effluent. 
 
(2)   Agricultural  Industry  may  include  an  enterprise  for  the  processing  and  packaging  of  the 
agricultural  products  that  are  produced  or  sourced  on  the  Property  or  elsewhere,  or  where 
processing in such proximity to the source is necessary, in the opinion of the Municipality, due to 
the nature, perishability and fragility of such agricultural produce. Agricultural Industries such as 
cold  storage  and  food  processing,  dairy,  mill  for  agricultural  produce,  water  bottling  plant, 
beverage plant, Micro-brewery, Micro-distillery, the Storage, sale and servicing of agricultural 
equipment shall be permitted. 
 
(3)    Abattoir and Noxious Industry shall be excluded. 
 
(4)    Clause 18(7) shall be applicable. 
 
AGRICULTURE 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for any farming activities, the cultivation of soil for growing of 
crops and rearing of animals, and one (1) Dwelling House. Land uses associated with farming 
activities include inter alia aqua-culture, bee farming, bird breeding, farming of cattle, goats, rabbits 
and sheep, game farming, greenhouse, sale and auctioning of farm animals, Market Gardens, 
Plant Nursery, plantations, mushroom production, forestry and orchards, and which produce is 
sourced, prepared and packaged on the Property.  
 
(2)   Agriculture may include Ancillary and Subservient uses such as Office, Storage and Dwelling Units 
for the farm manager and employees, of which no Dwelling Unit shall be sold as a sectional title 
scheme implicating an Illegal Township.  
 
(3)   Abattoirs,  Agricultural  Industry,  Animal  Boarding  Place,  Equestrian  Centre,  and  Sport  and 
Recreation Ground shall be excluded.  
 
AIRFIELD 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for landing and take-off, the Storage/hangars of aircraft and 
helicopters and may include Ancillary and Subservient Fuel Depot and Office, subject to the Civil 
Aviation Act, 2009 (Act 13 of 2009) as may be amended from time to time. 
 
(2)   Clause 18(8) shall be applicable. 
 
AIRPORT  
(1)   Means Land and Buildings designed or used for the landing and take-off of fixed wing and rotary 
wing  aircraft,  airways  control,  aircraft  hangars,  Fuel  Depot,  fuel  bays,  engine  run  test  area, 
training  facilities  for  flight  schools,  passenger  terminals,  luggage  and  freight  Storage  and 
handling, customs and migration control. 
 
(2)   Airport may include: 
(a)   ATM;

(b)   Backpackers; 
(c)   Banks; 
(d)   car rental facility;

vehicles, and

AIR RIGHTS 
(1)   Means a Building used for any land use which has been approved by the Municipality and which 
Building spans across a National Road or Provincial Road or Street at a specific height above 
the level of the National Road or Provincial Road or Street and which Building does not restrict 
the use of the affected National Road or Provincial Road or Street. 
 
(2)   Subterranean Rights shall be excluded. 
 
(3)   Clause 18(9) shall be applicable. 
 
ANIMAL BOARDING PLACE 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for the boarding and care of pet animals and includes breeding, 
training facilities and an animal rescue centre.  
 
(2)   Animal Boarding Place may include Ancillary and Subservient uses such as, but is not limited to: 
 
(a)   Offices; 
(b)   sale of animal related products; 
(c)   residence for staff; and 
(d)   treatment rooms. 
 
(3)   Clause 18(7) shall be applicable. 
 
APARTMENT BUILDING 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings consisting of Habitable Rooms used for residential occupation which 
shall include the following facilities: 
 
(a)   communal Kitchen or separate Kitchenettes; or both; and 
(b)   communal ablution facilities or separate bathrooms and toilets; or both. 
 
(2)   Apartment Building may include the following: 
 
(a)   communal dining room where meals are provided; 
(b)   Caretaker’s Flat;

(c)   Ancillary and Subservient communal facilities such as, but not limited to a laundry and 
vending machines for exclusive use of Occupants; and 
(d)   management by an Owner or manager or by a Place of Instruction or Institution, as may 
be determined by the Municipality. 
 
(3)   Clause 23(3) shall be applicable. 
 
AUCTIONEER 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for the Storage of new and used goods for sale to the public by 
means of an auction or over the counter. 
 
(2)   Auctioneer may include Ancillary and Subservient Office, including the duly appointed Sherriff’s 
office where goods are stored for auction. 
 
AUTO BODY REPAIR CENTRE 
(1)   Means  Land and  Buildings used  for  the  repair, removal,  installation  and  painting  of  integral 
component parts or the body of light vehicles, which have sustained minor damage. 
 
(2)   Auto Body Repair Centre may include:  
 
(a)   dent  removal  and  specialised  spray  painting,  provided  that  all  repair  work  shall  be 
conducted within the confines of an enclosed Building; 
 
(b)   all specialised spray-painting which shall be conducted within a dedicated enclosed spray-
painting booth with specialised air extraction and filtering apparatus to the satisfaction of 
the Municipality; and  
 
(c)   the placement, installation and use of machinery on the Property that radiates noise which 
noise  shall  be  subject  to  acoustical  requirements  and  screening  measures  to  the 
satisfaction of the Municipality. 
 
(3)   Clause 18(7) shall be applicable. 
 
AUTOMATIC TELLER MACHINE (ATM) 
Means Land and Buildings used for an automatic teller machine of a Bank or other financial institution. 
 
 
B 
 
BACKPACKERS 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings consisting of Habitable Rooms used by Guests and shall include 
communal facilities such as a Kitchen, dining room, lounge and ablution facilities. 
 
(2)   Backpackers may include a Caretaker’s Flat and dormitories. 
 
BAKERY 
Means Land and Buildings where food products are baked and manufactured in bulk for distribution to 
Shops, Warehouses and for Wholesale Trade. 
 
BANK 
Means Land and Buildings used as a public company registered provisionally or finally as a Bank in 
terms of the Deposit-taking Institutions Amendment Act, 1993 (Act 9 of 1993) as may be amended from 
time to time and may include an ATM.

BEAUTY SALON  
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for beauty treatment, body care and hairdressing for humans. 
 
(2)   Beauty Salon may include Ancillary and Subservient sale of related products. 
 
(3)   Shop shall be excluded. 
 
BIOFUEL PLANT 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for the production of heat, power and biofuels which include 
solid, liquid, or gaseous fuels that are derived from biomass. 
 
(2)   Biofuel Plant may include: 
 
(a)   infrastructure  associated  with  the  generation,  retention,  storage,  transmission  and 
distribution of electricity; and  
(b)   Ancillary and Subservient uses such as a Cafeteria, Guard House, Offices, Workshops, 
residence and Recreation Facility for the staff. 
 
BLOCK OF FLATS 
(1)   Means a Building, consisting of two (2) or more Dwelling Units, and more than one (1) Storey, 
that may be designed with a common entrance or foyer to the Buildings that gives access to the 
Dwelling Units. 
 
(2)   Block of Flats may include Ancillary and Subservient communal facilities such as, but not limited 
to, a laundry, post boxes and vending machines, for the exclusive use of the Occupants. 
 
(3)   Clause 23 shall be applicable to Properties zoned Residential 4. 
 
BOATHOUSE 
Means a Building used for the Storage and safekeeping of water vessels and water sport equipment. 
 
BREWERY 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for the manufacturing of beer: 
 
(a)   where the volume produced, in a calendar year, exceeds the thresholds of beer produced 
as provided for in the Liquor Act, 2003 (Act 59 of 2003) as may be amended from time to 
time; and 
 
(b)   includes brewing, refining, blending, bottling, packaging and processing of such beer. 
 
(2)   Brewery  may  include  a  Distribution  Centre  and  an  Ancillary  and  Subservient  Place  of 
Refreshment. 
 
BUILDER’S YARD 
Means Land and Buildings used for the Storage and sale of any new or used building materials and the 
rental  of  building  equipment  that  is  required  for  building  works  which  may  include  Ancillary  and 
Subservient Office.

CAFETERIA 
Means a Building or part of a Building, which is Ancillary and Subservient to the main use of the Building 
or  Property,  used  for  the  preparation  and sale  of  food  and  refreshments,  excluding  liquor,  for  the 
exclusive use of the employees, clients and customers.  
 
CALL CENTRE 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for telephonic or other electronic communication and a computer 
communication centre for receipt, electronic resolution and rerouting telephonic or other calls by 
means of call operators and helpdesks. 
 
(2)   Control Centre shall be excluded. 
 
CAMPING SITE 
Means  Land  and  Buildings used for camping  and  may  include  ablution  facilities, Caretaker’s  Flat, 
communal  Kitchen  and Ancillary and  Subservient  uses such as Place of  Refreshment, Recreation 
Facility and Shops.

25
CARETAKER’S FLAT 
Means  a  Dwelling  Unit  occupied  by  the  caretaker  who  is  responsible  for  the  maintenance  and 
supervision of the Land and Buildings on the same Property. 
 
CAR WASH 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for the washing, polishing and cleaning of vehicles by means of 
mechanical apparatus or by hand.  
 
(2)   Schedule 10 shall be applicable to Car Wash with reference to Table B, Column (3), as per the 
conditions and limitations contained in Schedule 10 per Use Zone. 
 
(3)   In certain Use Zones of Table B, specific land uses are listed in Column (3) which land uses are 
subject  to  certain  specific  conditions  and  only  these  land  uses  may  be  exercised  if  these 
conditions are complied with.  
 
CASINO 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for various forms of gambling. 
 
(2)   Casino may include a Conference Centre, Place of Amusement, Place of Refreshment and other 
Ancillary and Subservient uses. 
 
(3)   These Buildings shall comply with the noise zone criteria and acoustical screening requirements 
subject to Clause 18(7) and Clause 30(1). 
 
CEMETERY 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings designed or used for the burial of deceased humans and human 
ashes. 
 
(2)   Cemetery  may  include  Ancillary  and  Subservient  uses  such  as  a  Crematorium,  a  Wall  of 
Remembrance, a chapel, prayer area, funeral parlour, a Shop limited to the sale of convenience 
items only, Office and storerooms for the management of the Cemetery. 
 
(3)   Place of Public Worship (except for a chapel or prayer area), a Place of Refreshment and the 
sale of liquor shall be excluded. 
 
(4)   Clause 18(7) shall be applicable. 
 
CHANCELLERY 
(1)   Means  Land  and  Buildings  used  for  Offices  of  a  foreign  mission  for  diplomatic  or  related 
purposes. 
 
(2)   Chancellery may include Ancillary and Subservient Guard House and a visa office. 
 
CHILDREN'S HOME 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for the accommodation or occupation, care and education of 
orphans and children with special needs or circumstances, mental or physical disabilities, and/or 
who have been subject to physical or emotional trauma. 
 
(2)   Children’s Home may include Ancillary and Subservient facilities for the children and staff, such 
as residence for staff and Recreation Facility. 
 
CLINIC 
Means a Hospital for day patients with no overnight accommodation. 
 
CLUB HOUSE 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for gatherings by members of a club or an association and their 
guests.  

 
 
TSHWANE LAND USE SCHEME, 2024 
 
Adopted by virtue of Notice LA 652 of 2024:  08 May 2024  
Comes into operation:  01 July 2024 
                                                                             
 
 
26
 
(2)   Club House may include Ancillary and Subservient Office, Place of Refreshment and children’s 
play area. 
 
COMMERCIAL USE 
(1)   Means  Land  and  Buildings  used  for  Computer  Centre,  Distribution  Centre,  Laboratory,  Mini 
Public  Storage,  Storage,  Telecommunication  Centre,  Transport Depot,  Warehouse  and 
Wholesale Trade. 
 
(2)   Commercial Use may include a Cafeteria, a Caretaker’s Flat, Light Industry and Ancillary and 
Subservient Office to the main Commercial Use.  
 
COMMUNE 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings designed as a Dwelling House on a Property zoned Agricultural, 
Residential 1 and Undetermined, which is let and rented out to not more than six (6) Occupants, 
who share communal facilities. 
 
(2)   Commune may include a Caretaker’s Flat for the Owner or manager of the Commune. 
 
(3)   Home Enterprise subject to Schedule 9, shall be excluded. 
 
COMPUTER CENTRE 
(1)   Means  Land  and  Buildings used  for  the  storage,  processing,  programming  and providing  of 
electronic data. 
 
(2)   Computer Centre may include Ancillary and Subservient computer training, sale and repair of 
computers, printers and computer consumables and Storage.  
 
CONFERENCE CENTRE 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for congresses, seminars, training, meetings, cultural events 
and social activities.  
 
(2)   Conference Centre may include Ancillary and Subservient Cafeteria and Kitchen. 
 
(3)   Place of Amusement, Place of Refreshment and Place of Public Worship shall be excluded. 
 
(4)   The  Conference  Centre  shall  comply  with  the  noise  zone  criteria  and  acoustical  screening 
requirements subject to Clause 18(7), and Clause 30(1).  
 
CONSULATE  
Means an Embassy as defined. 
 
CONTROL CENTRE  
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used by emergency, security and safety units responsible daily for 24 
hours monitoring, analysing, action and tactical response to security and emergency situations. 
 
(2) Control Centre may include Ancillary and Subservient uses such as a Call Centre, fuel pump, 
security and emergency response vehicles and training facility. 
 
CREMATORIUM 
Means Land and Buildings used for the cremation of deceased human or animal tissue and may include 
Ancillary and Subservient Office.

D 
 
DISTILLERY 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for the manufacturing of spirits and wine: 
 
(a)   where the volume produced, in a calendar year, exceeds the thresholds of spirits and wine 
produced as provided for in the Liquor Act, 2003 (Act 59 of 2003) as may be amended 
from time to time; and 
 
(b)   includes the distilling, refining, blending, bottling, packaging and processing of such spirits 
and wine. 
 
(2)   Distillery  may  include  a  Distribution  Centre  and  an  Ancillary  and  Subservient  Place  of 
Refreshment. 
 
DISTRIBUTION CENTRE 
Means Warehouse or other Building from where goods are distributed and may include a Transport 
Depot. 
 
DRIVE THRU RESTAURANT 
Means Land and Buildings used for the preparation and sale of food and refreshments and is designed 
for the purpose of customers purchasing such items at a counter, or through a window from their 
vehicles and may include the consumption of such purchased food and refreshments on the Property.  
 
DUPLEX DWELLING 
Means a Dwelling Unit as defined. 
 
DWELLING HOUSE 
(1)   Means one (1) Dwelling Unit on a Property zoned Agricultural, Residential 1 or Undetermined.  
 
(2)   A Dwelling House may include the letting of any part of the Dwelling House and its Outbuildings 
by an Owner or Occupant of a Dwelling House, provided that not more than two (2) bedrooms for 
a maximum of two (2) persons are so let. 
 
DWELLING UNIT 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for residential occupation which Buildings shall consist of the 
following self-contained suite of rooms internally and mutually connected: 
 
(a)   Habitable Room(s); 
(b)   bathroom(s); 
(c)   toilet(s); and  
(d)   not more than one (1) Kitchen without the Permission of the Municipality. 
 
(2)   Dwelling Unit may include: 
 
(a)   Ancillary and Subservient Outbuildings; and  
(b)   a Home Enterprise subject to Schedule 9.

EMBASSY 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used as the official residence of a consul or ambassador or other 
chief of a diplomatic mission.

(2)   Embassy may include Ancillary and Subservient Guard House and Office.

EQUESTRIAN CENTRE

(2)   Equestrian  Centre  may  include  Cafeteria,  competitions,  equestrian shows  and Ancillary  and 
Subservient sale of related products. 
 
(3)   Shop shall be excluded. 
 
 
F 
 
FARM STORE 
Means Land and Buildings used for the sale of agricultural produce, animal feed, convenience items, 
refreshments and take-aways, on a Property zoned Agricultural, Municipal and Undetermined, provided 
that: 
 
(1)   the area of the Building shall not exceed 60 m²; 
 
(2)   the Farm Store shall be situated at least ten (10) metres from any Property boundary; and  
 
(3)   the sale of liquor shall be excluded. 
 
FILLING STATION 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for the storage and retail sale of fuels, energy and lubricants. 
 
(2)   Filling Station may include:  
 
(a)   a Shop limited to the sale of convenience items only; 
(b)   Office; 
(c)   Kitchen and storeroom;  
(d)   one working bay for the emergency repair of vehicles; 
(e)   ATM; 
(f)    safe or deposit boxes for delivery of parcels and packages; and  
(g)   the sale of liquified petroleum gas (LP Gas). 
 
(3)   The sale of liquor shall be excluded. 
 
(4)   Clause 24 shall be applicable. 
 
FITNESS CENTRE 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings where people exercise (also referred to as a gym). 
 
(2)   Fitness Centre may include Ancillary and Subservient Place of Refreshment and sale of fitness 
related products. 
 
(3)   Shop shall be excluded. 
 
FLEA MARKET  
Means Land and Buildings used for the display and sale of products, food, refreshments and beverages 
including farmers’ market and fresh produce.

FUEL DEPOT

FUNERAL UNDERTAKER  
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for funeral arrangements for deceased humans. 
 
(2)   Funeral Undertaker may include: 
 
(a)   a  funeral  parlour  where  the  deceased  are  prepared  for  burial  or  cremation,  including 
refrigeration rooms and storage; 
(b)   display and sale of coffins, gravestones, flowers and other related products; 
(c)   Office; 
(d)   Place of Public Worship, restricted to a chapel or prayer area only; 
(e)   waiting and viewing rooms; and  
(f)    Ancillary and Subservient Cafeteria and Caretaker’s Flat. 
 
(3)   Crematorium and Mortuary shall be excluded. 
 
(4)   Clause 18(7) shall be applicable.  
 
 
G 
 
GARDEN CENTRE 
(1)   Means  Land  and  Buildings  used  for  the  cultivation  of  plants,  sale  of  plants,  fish  and  birds, 
gardening products and related accessories.  
 
(2)   Garden Centre may include Ancillary and Subservient Place of Refreshment and Storage. 
 
GOVERNMENT PURPOSES 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used by or on behalf of any organ of state or associated state-owned 
entities, for the execution of its powers, functions and duties assigned to any organ of state or 
state-owned entity in terms of either the Constitution of the Republic of South Africa, 1996, or 
any other relevant legislation and includes reference to Public Service Infrastructure. 
 
(2)   Government Purposes may include: 
 
(a)   Clinic; 
(b)   correctional facilities; 
(c)   courts of law; 
(d)   depots; 
(e)   Hospital; 
(f)    libraries and archives; 
(g)   Office;

(i)    post offices; 
(j)    Place of Child Care; 
(k)   Place of Instruction; 
(l)    Plant Nursery; 
(m)   Public Open Space; 
(n)   Tourist Facilities; and  
(o)   Workshop.

(3)   Industry and Noxious Industry shall be excluded. 
 
GUARD HOUSE 
(1)   Means a Building for controlling access to a Property, which may contain security equipment and 
related documents used by guards. 
 
(2)   A Guard House may include ablution facilities and a Kitchenette for the exclusive use of the 
guards in the Building as well as an Ancillary and Subservient Office. 
 
(3)   Control Centre shall be excluded. 
 
GUEST HOUSE  
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used by Guests and shall include: 
 
(a)   a maximum of 16 bedrooms for a maximum of 32 Guests; 
(b)   a dining room, lounge and leisure amenities that are for communal use; and 
(c)   a residence for the Owner or manager who shall manage the Guest House. 
 
(2)   Guest House may include:  
 
(a)   Kitchenette in each bedroom;  
(b)   staff accommodation; and 
(c)   Ancillary and Subservient uses such as a bar and Conference Centre for the exclusive use 
of such Guests. 
 
(3)   Guest House shall exclude: 
 
(a)   Adult Premises; 
(b)   Health Spa; 
(c)   Place of Amusement;  
(d)   Place of Refreshment, except a bar as referred to in (2)(c) above; 
(e)   Self-catering Units; and 
(f)    Social Hall. 
 
 
H 
 
HEALTH SPA 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for beauty treatment, body care and hairdressing for humans. 
 
(2)   Health Spa may include Ancillary and Subservient facilities such as overnight accommodation 
for patrons, residence for staff and the sale of related beauty products.  
 
HELIPAD 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings designed or used for the landing and taking off of helicopters and may 
include a terminal for passengers. 
 
(2)   Clause 18(8) shall be applicable. 
 
HOME ENTERPRISE 
Means  the  practice  of  an  activity,  business,  hobby  or  occupation  in  a  Dwelling  Unit,  including 
Outbuildings, with the aim of deriving an income therefrom, subject to Schedule 9. 
 
HOSPITAL 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for the accommodation and care of sick or injured humans or 
humans needing specialised medical treatment or operations.

(2)   Hospital may include operating theatres, X-ray rooms, and Ancillary and Subservient uses such

HOTEL

INDUSTRY

INSTITUTION 
Means Land and Buildings, whether public or private, used for the care or treatment of humans, which

Home, and may include overnight facilities and residence for staff.

LABORATORY 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for scientific and medical research, testing and experimenting. 
Any activities that create a danger or nuisance of noise, smoke, fumes or smell are excluded.

LIGHT INDUSTRY

Light  Industry  with  reference  to  Table  B,  Column  (3),  as  per  the  conditions  and  limitations 
contained in Schedule 10 per Use Zone. 
 
(5)   In certain Use Zones of Table B, specific land uses are listed in Column (3) which are subject to 
certain specific conditions and only these land uses may be exercised if those conditions are 
complied with.

technician and prosthetist.

(a)   where the volume produced in a calendar year, shall not exceed the thresholds of beer

MORTUARY

MUNICIPAL INFRASTRUCTURE SERVICES  
Means Land and Buildings used for municipal services as defined in the LUM By-law. 
 
MUNICIPAL PURPOSES 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for the execution of any power, functions and duties assigned 
to a Municipality in terms of the Constitution of the Republic of South Africa, 1996 or any other 
law and include Municipal Infrastructure Services as defined.  
 
(2)   Municipal Purposes may include: 
 
(a)   Cafeteria; 
(b)   Clinic; 
(c)   libraries; 
(d)   Office; 
(e)   Place of Instruction; 
(f)    Plant Nursery; 
(g)   Public Open Space; 
(h)   Sport and Recreation Ground;  
(i)    Tourist Facilities; and 
(j)    Workshop. 
 
MUNICIPAL TRANSITIONAL SETTLEMENT 
Means Land used for the settlement of persons in temporary or emergency housing and the provision 
of Ancillary and Subservient structures and services while permanent housing is being formalised in 
terms of the relevant legislation, subject to Schedule 16.  
 
 
N 
 
NATIONAL ROADS 
Means a Road as defined in the National Road Traffic Act, 1996 (Act 93 of 1996) as may be amended 
from time to time.  
 
NIGHT CLUB 
Means  Land  and  Buildings  used  for  a  combination  of  a  Place  of  Refreshment  and  a  Place  of 
Amusement. 
 
NOXIOUS INDUSTRY 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for the production and processing or any activities such as those 
listed in Schedule 8, that causes the discharge of noxious substances, dust, effluvia, gasses, 
noise, smells, smoke, vapour or waste matter that causes environmental- and health nuisances. 
 
(2)   Noxious Industry may include a Caretaker’s Flat. 
 
(3)   Clauses 14(7) and 18(7) shall be applicable. 
 
NURSING HOME 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for medical and psychiatric care and treatment of ill, injured, 
frail, mentally or physically disabled persons or persons who need post-operative care, and the 
rehabilitation of ill persons or persons with addiction. 
 
(2)   Nursing  Home  may  include  Ancillary  and  Subservient  Caretaker’s  Flat,  Medical  Consulting 
Rooms, Place of Refreshment and Shop. 
 
(3)   Operating rooms and the sale of liquor shall be excluded.

36
 
O 
 
OCCASIONAL USE 
Means Land and Buildings used once a month for a maximum continuous period of 72 hours within a 
calendar month for uses as stipulated in Clause 17(2). 
 
OFFICE 
(1)   Means  Land  and  Buildings  used  for  professional,  clerical,  administrative,  management, 
marketing and consulting services and a Chancellery. 
 
(2)   Office may include Ancillary and Subservient Cafeteria. 
 
(3)   Control Centre and Medical Consulting Rooms shall be excluded. 
 
OPEN SPACE 
Means open space as defined in the LUM By-law.  
 
OUTBUILDING  
(1)   Means Ancillary and Subservient Buildings to the main Building on the Property, which have its 
own entrances or doors and have no interleading door to the main Building, but which are attached 
to or free standing from the main Building. 
 
(2)   Outbuildings may be used for residential accommodation, up to a maximum of 50 m² which may 
consist of Habitable Rooms, bathroom(s) and only one (1) kitchen, provided that: 
 
(a)   the maximum of 50 m² may be increased with the Permission of the Municipality up to a 
maximum of 20% of the Net Floor Area (NFA) of the main Building; and  
 
(b)   the residential accommodation may not be sold as a sectional title scheme.  
 
(3)   All Outbuildings, excluding carports, shall not exceed 50% of the NFA of the main Building, but 
may be increased with the Permission of the Municipality. 
 
(4)   The restrictions under paragraphs (2)(a) and (3) above shall not be applicable to Agricultural and 
Undetermined zoned Properties. 
 
 
P 
 
PANEL BEATER 
Means Land and Buildings used for the replacement, repair and spray-painting of the bodywork of 
vehicles, subject to Clause 18(7). 
 
PARKING GARAGE 
(1)   Means  Land  and  Buildings  used  for  an  automated,  semi-automated,  manually  controlled  or 
mechanical structure designed or used for the parking of vehicles, not being for trade or sale, 
which  is  not  required  or  utilised  for  the  parking  requirements for  the  main  use  on  the  same 
Property, but for a use on another Property. 
 
(2)   Motor Workshop shall be excluded.  
 
PARKING SITE 
Means Land and Buildings used solely for the parking of vehicles, excluding busses and trucks, not being 
for sale or trade and may include a Guard House. 

 
 
TSHWANE LAND USE SCHEME, 2024 
 
Adopted by virtue of Notice LA 652 of 2024:  08 May 2024  
Comes into operation:  01 July 2024 
                                                                             
 
 
37
 
PEDESTRIAN BRIDGE 
(1)   Means a  bridge or underground subway, providing access for non-motorised transport only, 
except for motorised wheelchairs, across or underneath Streets, railways, National Roads and 
Provincial Roads, linking Buildings or Properties or road reserves on either side of the Streets, 
railways, National Roads and Provincial Roads, to the satisfaction of the Municipality read with 
the provisions of section 63 of the Local Government Ordinance,1939 (Ordinance 17 of 1939) as 
may be amended from time to time and shall be regarded as Public Service Infrastructure. 
 
(2)   Pedestrian Bridge shall exclude any other land use. 
 
PETTING ZOO 
(1)   Means  Land  and  Buildings  used  for  the  keeping  and  breeding  of  animals  for  display  and 
interaction with persons visiting the Property. 
 
(2)   Petting Zoo may include a children’s play area, outdoor recreation area for functions and Place 
of Refreshment. 
 
PICNIC PLACE 
Means Land and Buildings used for outdoor recreation such as picnics and braais and may include 
Ancillary and Subservient uses. 
 
PLACE OF AMUSEMENT 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for entertainment purposes, such as, but is not limited to: 
 
(a)   amusement park; 
(b)   cinema; 
(c)   concert hall; 
(d)   dancing; 
(e)   electronic games or slot machines or limited pay-out gambling machines; 
(f)    exhibition hall; 
(g)   gambling; 
(h)   music hall; 
(i)    outdoor arena used for live concerts, performances or sport; 
(j)    skating rink; 
(k)   table games; and 
(l)    Theatre. 
 
(2)   Place  of  Amusement  shall  comply  with  the  noise  zone  criteria  and  acoustical  screening 
requirements subject to Clause 18(7) and Clause 30(1). 
 
PLACE OF CHILD CARE 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for the admission, protection and temporary or partial care of 
more than six (6) children up to the age of 18 years, away from their parents or guardians.  
 
(a)   Depending on the registration of a Place of Child Care, it can admit babies, toddlers, pre-
primary school aged children and school going children.  
 
(b)   The care for children may be on a full day or other basis, such as after school care. 
 
(2)   Place of Instruction, only for pre-primary school education, may be conducted.  
 
(3)   Apartment Building, Institution, overnight accommodation for children and a Place of Instruction 
shall be excluded. 
 
 
 

 
 
TSHWANE LAND USE SCHEME, 2024 
 
Adopted by virtue of Notice LA 652 of 2024:  08 May 2024  
Comes into operation:  01 July 2024 
                                                                             
 
 
38
PLACE OF DAY CARE FOR THE AGED 
Means Land and Buildings used for care of persons older than 55 years who are not able to care for 
themselves during the day but excludes overnight care and accommodation for such persons. 
 
PLACE OF INSTRUCTION  
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for educational purposes such as, but is not limited to: 
 
(a)   an academy; 
(b)   art gallery; 
(c)   college; 
(d)   convent; 
(e)   lecture hall; 
(f)    library; 
(g)   monastery; 
(h)   museum; 
(i)    school; 
(j)    technical institute; and 
(k)   Tertiary Institution. 
 
(2)   Place of Instruction may include Ancillary and Subservient uses such as Apartment Building, 
Cafeteria, Clubhouse, Conference Centre, Fitness Centre, Internet Café, Laboratory, Place of 
Child Care, Sport and Recreation Ground and Tourist Facilities. 
 
PLACE OF PUBLIC WORSHIP 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for religious purposes. 
 
(2)   Place  of  Public  Worship  may  include  Ancillary  and  Subservient  ablution  facilities,  social, 
educational and recreational activities and one (1) Dwelling Unit. 
 
(3)   Funeral Undertaker, Wall of Remembrance and Cemetery shall be excluded. 
 
(4)   Clause 18(7) shall be applicable. 
 
PLACE OF REFRESHMENT 
(1)   Means Land and Buildings used for the preparation and sale of food and refreshments. The 
consumption of such food and refreshment shall take place on the Property, except for a Drive 
Thru Restaurant and for take-aways where the consumption could be on or off the Property. 
 
(2)   Place of Refreshment may include uses such as, but is not limited to: 
 
(a)   Drive Thru Restaurant; 
(b)   children’s play area; 
(c)   Roadhouse; 
(d)   take-aways; 
(e)   television  screens  and  soft  background  music,  which  shall  not be  audible  outside  the 
boundaries of the Property; and 
(f)    Ancillary and Subservient entertainment restricted to a maximum of five (5) dartboards, 
five  (5)  table  games,  five  (5)  electronic  games  and  five  (5)  limited  pay-out  gambling 
machines. 
 
(3)   Live music and a Place of Amusement shall be excluded. 
 
(4)   Clause 18(7) shall be applicable. 
 
PLANT NURSERY 
Means Land and Buildings used for the cultivation and Storage of plants and may include an Ancillary 
and Subservient Shop.

39
 
POWER STATION  
Means  Land  and  Buildings  used  for  the  generating  of  electricity  and  may  include  Ancillary  and 
Subservient uses. 
 
PRIVATE OPEN SPACE 
Means Open Space as defined to which the general public has no right of access. 
 
PRIVATE ROAD 
Means a Private Street as defined. 
 
PRIVATE STREET 
(1)   Means a Street on private Property, whether registered as a separate Property or servitude area, 
to which the general public has not obtained a common right of access, of which the control, 
maintenance and management thereof has not vested in the Municipality, that is nominally used 
as a street or roadway either through ownership or through the registration of a right of way in 
favour of any Property or Person, and shall be approved as access for purposes of exercising 
the rights to the satisfaction of the Municipality, and shall be read with the provisions of the LUM 
By-law. 
 
(2)   A Private Street may include Access Control. 
 
(3)   The granting of any right of way in favour of the Municipality over such Private Street shall not be 
regarded as having granted any right of access to the general public. 
 
PROVINCIAL ROADS 
Means a road as defined in the Gauteng Transport Infrastructure Act, 2001 (Act 8 of 2001) as may be 
amended from time to time. 
 
PUBLIC GARAGE 
(1)   Means a Filling Station as defined. 
 
(2)   Public Garage may include an Ancillary and Subservient Motor Workshop and Vehicle Sales 
Showroom.  
 
(3)   Panel Beater and Auto Body Repair Centre shall be excluded. 
 
(4)   Clause 24 shall be applicable. 
 
PUBLIC OPEN SPACE  
Means any Open Space as defined and vested in the Municipality to which the general public has right 
of access.  
 
PUBLIC ROAD 
Means a Public Street as defined. 
 
PUBLIC STREET 
Means a Street as defined in the Local Government Ordinance, 1939 (Ordinance 17 of 1939) as may 
be amended from time to time, read with section 63 thereof and shall include any road or roadway 
zoned for the purposes of a road or street, that is nominally used as a street or road, whether on public 
or private Property, read with the definitions as contained in the LUM By-law. For purposes of the 
determination of public participation and abutting ownership, a National Road or Provincial Road shall 
be excluded.
